\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a11720c99295aa0f86c41ad6f2108d0b9}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a11720c99295aa0f86c41ad6f2108d0b9}} 
void {\bfseries webgl\+Not\+Available} ()
\end{DoxyCompactItemize}
\begin{Indent}\textbf{ GL methods}\par
{\em The GL methods are mostly 1-\/on-\/1 translated to the identical Java\+Script call in Web\+GL. You can use the GL methods in your \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}} specializations. \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt}{Wt}} takes care that data, arguments, ... are transfered to the client side and that the equivalent Java\+Script Web\+GL funtion is executed when using client-\/side rendering. When using server-\/side rendering, the appropriate Open\+GL functions are called. }\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}

\doxysubsection*{Additional Inherited Members}


\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
GL support class. 

The \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}} class is an interface to the H\+T\+M\+L5 Web\+GL infrastructure for client-\/side rendering, and Open\+GL for server-\/side rendering. Its A\+PI is based on the Web\+GL A\+PI. To fully understand Web\+GL, it is recommended to read the Web\+GL standard in addition to this documentation.

The most recent version of the Web\+GL specification can be found here\+: \href{http://www.khronos.org/registry/webgl/specs/latest/1.0/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+khronos.\+org/registry/webgl/specs/latest/1.\+0/}}

The goal of the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}} class is to provide a method to render 3D structures in the browser, where rendering and rerendering is normally done at the client side in Java\+Script without interaction from the server, in order to obtain a smooth user interaction. Unless the scene requires server-\/side updates, there is no communication with the server.

The rendering interface resembles to Open\+GL ES, the same standard as Web\+GL is based on. This is a stripped down version of the normal Open\+GL as we usually find them on desktops. Many stateful Open\+GL features are not present in Open\+GL ES\+: no modelview and camera transformation stacks, no default lighting models, no support for other rendering methods than through V\+B\+Os, ... Therefore much existing example code for Open\+GL applications and shaders will not work on Web\+GL without modifications. The \textquotesingle{}learning webgl\textquotesingle{} web site at \href{http://learningwebgl.com/}{\texttt{ http\+://learningwebgl.\+com/}} is a good starting point to get familiar with Web\+GL.

To use a W\+G\+L\+Widget, you must derive from it and reimplement the painter methods. Usually, you will always need to implement \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}}. Optionally, you may choose to implement \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}} (if your widget does not have a fixed size), and \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}}. If you need to modify the painting methods, a repaint is triggered by calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a18d874bacc0cf315da7c9eff2867314a}{repaint\+G\+L()}} method. The default behaviour for any of these four painting functions is to do nothing.

The four painter methods (\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}}) all record Java\+Script which is sent to the browser. The Java\+Script code of \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}} is cached client-\/side, and may be executed many times, e.\+g. to repaint a scene from different viewpoints. The Java\+Script code of \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}} are intended for Open\+GL state updates, and is therefore only executed once on the client and is then discarded.

There are four painting methods that you may implement in a specialization of this class. The purpose of these functions is to register what Java\+Script code has to be executed to render a scene. Through invocations of the Web\+GL functions documented below, Wt records the Java\+Script calls that have to be invoked in the browser. 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}}}}\+: this function is executed after the GL context has been initialized. It is also executed when the {\ttfamily webglcontextrestored} signal is fired. You can distinguish between the first initialization and restoration of context using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a95701ef1dc1da6a694da630daba35b5e}{restoring\+Context()}}. This is the ideal location to compose shader programs, send V\+BO\textquotesingle{}s to the client, extract uniform and attribute locations, ... Due to the presence of V\+BO\textquotesingle{}s, this function may generate a large amount of data to the client. 
\item {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}}}}\+: this function is executed whenever the canvas dimensions change. A change in canvas size will require you to invoke the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_aa7eef06c55522565ae86d9d84ebcbf79}{viewport()}} function again, as well as recalculate the projection matrices (especially when the aspect ratio has changed). The \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}} function is therefore the ideal location to set those properties. The \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}} function is invoked automatically on every resize, and after the first \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}} invocation. Additional invocations may be triggered by calling repaint() with the R\+E\+S\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+GL flag. 
\item {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}}}}\+: this is the main scene drawing function. Through its execution, Wt records what has to be done to render a scene, and it is executed every time that the scene is to be redrawn. You can use the V\+BO\textquotesingle{}s and shaders prepared in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}} phase. Usually, this function sets uniforms and attributes, links attributes to V\+BO\textquotesingle{}s, applies textures, and draws primitives. You may also create local programs, buffers, ... Remember that this function is executed a lot of times, so every buffer/program created in this function should also be destroyed to avoid memory leaks. This function is transmitted once to the client, and is executed when the scene needs to be redrawn. Redraws may be triggered from mouse events, timer triggers, events on e.\+g. a video element, or whatever other event. The \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}} function can be updated through invoking \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a18d874bacc0cf315da7c9eff2867314a}{repaint\+G\+L()}} with the P\+A\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+GL flag. 
\item {\bfseries{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}}}}\+: V\+BO\textquotesingle{}s, programs, uniforms, GL properties, or anything else set during intialize\+G\+L() are not necessarily immutable. If you want to change, add, remove or reconfigure those properties, the execution of an \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}} function can be triggered by invoking \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a18d874bacc0cf315da7c9eff2867314a}{repaint\+G\+L()}} with the U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+GL flag. This signals that \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}} needs to be evaluated -\/ just once. It is possible that the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}} function also requires updates as consequence of the changes in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}} function; in this case, you should also set the P\+A\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+GL flag of \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a18d874bacc0cf315da7c9eff2867314a}{repaint\+G\+L()}}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

The GL functions are intended to be used exclusively from within the invocation of the four callback functions mentioned above. In order to manually trigger the execution of these function, use the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a18d874bacc0cf315da7c9eff2867314a}{repaint\+G\+L()}}.

A \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}} must be given a size explicitly, or must be put inside a layout manager that manages its width and height. The behaviour of a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}} that was not given a size is undefined.

\doxyparagraph*{Binary buffer transfers}

In \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a2f58fba9828fe37c00dd393c37200c11}{buffer\+Datafv()}}, there is an additional boolean argument where you can indicate that you want the data to be transferred to the client in binary form. A \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WMemoryResource}{W\+Memory\+Resource}} is created for each of these buffers. If you know all previous resources are not required in the client anymore, you can free memory with the method \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a63d0821e22a8519e347d2e21aa3bf0ab}{clear\+Binary\+Resources()}} (the memory is also managed, so this is not neccesary). If you want to manage these resources entirely by yourself, the following method can be used.

Using create\+And\+Load\+Array\+Buffer(), you can load an array buffer in binary format from an U\+RL. This will cause the client to fetch the given U\+RL, and make the contents of the file available in an \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1ArrayBuffer}{Array\+Buffer}}, which can then be used by Buffer\+Data() to bind them to an Open\+GL buffer. This is ideal to load V\+BO buffers in a faster way, as it avoids converting floats to text strings on the server and then back to floats on the client. You can combine this with the use of \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WResource}{W\+Resource}} (e.\+g. \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WMemoryResource}{W\+Memory\+Resource}}) to send an std\+::vector of vertices to the client. \mbox{\hyperlink{classNote}{Note}} that using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1ArrayBuffer}{Array\+Buffer}} is not possible when you want a fall-\/back in the form of server-\/side rendering.

\doxyparagraph*{Client side matrices and vectors.}

The \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}} provides the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1JavaScriptMatrix4x4}{W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::\+Java\+Script\+Matrix4x4}} class as a mechanism to use client-\/side modifiable matrices in the render functions. These matrices can be used identically to the \textquotesingle{}constant\textquotesingle{}, with the advantage that there is no need to have a roundtrip to the server to redraw the scene when they are changed. As such, they are ideal for mouse-\/based camera manipulations, timer triggered animations, or object manipulations.

There\textquotesingle{}s also support for client-\/side modifiable vectors, with \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1JavaScriptVector}{W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::\+Java\+Script\+Vector}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::add\+Java\+Script\+Vector (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1JavaScriptVector}{Java\+Script\+Vector}} \&}]{v }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Register a vector with this \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}. 

You can call this outside of \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}} methods. After a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1JavaScriptVector}{Java\+Script\+Vector}} is added to a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}, its \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WWidget_a83a186d2feacfbfbdb5b54f4cefc6735}{js\+Ref()}} becomes valid, and can be used in a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1JSlot}{J\+Slot}}, for example. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_adf0be3425f753dc1cca94a4a8230db5a}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_adf0be3425f753dc1cca94a4a8230db5a}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::buffer\+Data (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ae94560816975bedd91b9d63fc4b710a8}{G\+Lenum}}}]{target,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1ArrayBuffer}{Array\+Buffer}}}]{res,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ae94560816975bedd91b9d63fc4b710a8}{G\+Lenum}}}]{usage }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



gl\+Buffer\+Data -\/ create and initialize a buffer object\textquotesingle{}s data store from an \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1ArrayBuffer}{Array\+Buffer}} 

Set the size and contents of the currently bound Web\+G\+L\+Buffer object to be a copy of the given \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1ArrayBuffer}{Array\+Buffer}}.

\href{http://www.khronos.org/opengles/sdk/2.0/docs/man/xhtml/glBufferData.xml}{\texttt{ gl\+Buffer\+Data() Open\+GL ES manpage}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classNote}{Note}}\+: an \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1ArrayBuffer}{Array\+Buffer}} refers to a javascript object, which cannot be used for server-\/side rendering. If a server-\/side fallback will be used, then \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a2f58fba9828fe37c00dd393c37200c11}{buffer\+Datafv()}} should be used with the additional boolean argument to indicate binary transfer of the data in case of client-\/side rendering.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bufferDatafv()}{bufferDatafv()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Iterator $>$ \\
void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::buffer\+Datafv (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ae94560816975bedd91b9d63fc4b710a8}{G\+Lenum}}}]{target,  }\item[{const Iterator}]{begin,  }\item[{const Iterator}]{end,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ae94560816975bedd91b9d63fc4b710a8}{G\+Lenum}}}]{usage,  }\item[{bool}]{binary = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



GL function that loads float or double data in a V\+BO. 

Unlike the C version, we can\textquotesingle{}t accept a void $\ast$ here. We must be able to interpret the buffer\textquotesingle{}s data in order to transmit it to the JS side.

Later we may also want versions with strides and offsets to cope with more complex buffer layouts that we typically see on desktop Web\+GL apps; suggestions to improve this are welcome

\mbox{\hyperlink{classNote}{Note}}\+: prefer \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a6c9c9445925ae2ed49583750259ec49e}{buffer\+Datafv(\+G\+Lenum target, const std\+::vector$<$float$>$ \&buffer, G\+Lenum usage, bool binary)}}

\href{http://www.khronos.org/opengles/sdk/2.0/docs/man/xhtml/glBufferData.xml}{\texttt{ gl\+Buffer\+Data() Open\+GL ES manpage}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a6c9c9445925ae2ed49583750259ec49e}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a6c9c9445925ae2ed49583750259ec49e}}

Initialize a buffer object\textquotesingle{}s data store from an \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1ArrayBuffer}{Array\+Buffer}}. 

Load the data of the currently bound Web\+G\+L\+Buffer object from the given \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1ArrayBuffer}{Array\+Buffer}}. The first byte of the resource data will be written at the given offset of the currently bound buffer.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::clear\+Binary\+Resources (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



remove all binary buffer resources 

Removes all W\+Memory\+Resources that were allocated when calling buffer\+Datafv with binary=true. This is not required, since the resources are also managed, but if you are sure they will not be used anymore in the client, this can help free some memory. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a75296a47dc94ea8de2d7256ba179c0e9}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a75296a47dc94ea8de2d7256ba179c0e9}}

Create a matrix that can be manipulated in client-\/side Java\+Script. 

This is a shorthand for creating a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1JavaScriptMatrix4x4}{Java\+Script\+Matrix4x4}}, then adding it to a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}} with add\+Java\+Script\+Matrix4, and initializing it with init\+Java\+Script\+Matrix4.

This method should only be called in \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af19547c0b3607cb7746a1ccde3590bec}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af19547c0b3607cb7746a1ccde3590bec}}

Create a vector of a certain length that can be manipulated in client-\/side Java\+Script. 

This is a shorthand for creating a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1JavaScriptVector}{Java\+Script\+Vector}}, then adding it to a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}} with add\+Java\+Script\+Vector, and initializing it with init\+Java\+Script\+Vector.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{enableClientErrorChecks()}{enableClientErrorChecks()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::enable\+Client\+Error\+Checks (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{enable = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



enable client-\/side error messages (read detailed doc!) 

This option will add client-\/side code to check the result of every Web\+GL call, and will popup an error dialog if a Web\+GL call returned an error. The Java\+Script then invokes the client-\/side debugger. This code is intended to test your application, and should not be used in production. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a0cd5dd8da88aa9ba942d0ff778edacb4}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a0cd5dd8da88aa9ba942d0ff778edacb4}}

\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!initializeGL@{initializeGL}}
\index{initializeGL@{initializeGL}!Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{initializeGL()}{initializeGL()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::initialize\+GL (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Initialize the GL state when the widget is first shown. 

\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}} is called when the widget is first rendered, and when the webglcontextrestored signal is fired. You can distinguish between the first initialization and context restoration using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a95701ef1dc1da6a694da630daba35b5e}{restoring\+Context()}}. It usually creates most of the GL related state\+: shaders, V\+B\+Os, uniform locations, ...

If this state is to be updated during the lifetime of the widget, you should specialize the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}} to accomodate for this. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesian3DChart_af8c1d06f76d31fadc830e529e8170c0f}{Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian3\+D\+Chart}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classPaintWidget_ac159afb73949f18af2fa21afb53377fb}{Paint\+Widget}}.

Initialize the client-\/side Java\+Script for the given \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1JavaScriptMatrix4x4}{Java\+Script\+Matrix4x4}}. 

If the given matrix is not associated with a widget yet, it will be added to this widget.

If the given matrix has already been added to a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}, then this \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}} should be the same as the one you call init\+Java\+Script\+Matrix4 on.

This method should only be called in \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a0641829db6e4a27077fd72f1c9e543b1}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a0641829db6e4a27077fd72f1c9e543b1}}

\href{http://www.khronos.org/opengles/sdk/2.0/docs/man/xhtml/glLinkProgram.xml}{\texttt{ gl\+Link\+Program() Open\+GL ES manpage}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}} 
\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!paintGL@{paintGL}}
\index{paintGL@{paintGL}!Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{paintGL()}{paintGL()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::paint\+GL (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Update the client-\/side painting function. 

This method is invoked client-\/side when a repaint is required, i.\+e. when the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ab44c8692c63dd82a2b5bcf70961319c5}{repaint\+Slot()}} (a Java\+Script-\/side \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1JSlot}{J\+Slot}}) is triggered. Typical examples are\+: after mouse-\/based camera movements, after a timed update of a camera or an object\textquotesingle{}s position, after a resize event (\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}} will also be called then), after an animation event, ... In many cases, this function will be executed client-\/side many many times.

Using the GL functions from this class, you construct a scene. The implementation tracks all Java\+Script calls that need to be performed to draw the scenes, and will replay them verbatim on every trigger of the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ab44c8692c63dd82a2b5bcf70961319c5}{repaint\+Slot()}}. There are a few mechanisms that may be employed to change what is rendered without updating the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}} cache\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Client-\/side matrices may be used to change camera viewpoints, manipilate separate object\textquotesingle{}s model transformation matrices, ...  
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1Shader}{Shader}} sources can be updated without requiring the paint function to be renewed 
\end{DoxyItemize}

Updating the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}} cache is usually not too expensive; the V\+B\+Os, which are large in many cases, are already at the client side, while the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}} code only draws the V\+B\+Os. Of course, if you have to draw many separate objects, the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}} JS code may become large and updating is more expensive.

In order to update the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}} cache, call \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a18d874bacc0cf315da7c9eff2867314a}{repaint\+G\+L()}} with the P\+A\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+GL parameter, which will cause the invocation of this method. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesian3DChart_a0be4fb12f72c2d6eb7679d7eda83028d}{Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian3\+D\+Chart}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{classPaintWidget_a8db0bbabdd863bdd8630c49b26f9b43f}{Paint\+Widget}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a232ef15851eb0c3b9c202ec9ab851fb4}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a232ef15851eb0c3b9c202ec9ab851fb4}}

\href{http://www.khronos.org/opengles/sdk/2.0/docs/man/xhtml/glPolygonOffset.xml}{\texttt{ gl\+Polygon\+Offset() Open\+GL ES manpage}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a1175690b649a3107cab1084e770d6ce2}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a1175690b649a3107cab1084e770d6ce2}} 
\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!render@{render}}
\index{render@{render}!Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{render()}{render()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::render (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WFlags}{W\+Flags}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_a1097ddb5b58c20fe2f6c9d096e71575c}{Render\+Flag}} $>$}]{flags }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Renders the widget. 

This function renders the widget (or an update for the widget), after this has been scheduled using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WWidget_a5d3d4edaafa2d7c892a5078f3df4cf11}{schedule\+Render()}}.

The default implementation will render the widget by serializing changes to Java\+Script and H\+T\+ML. You may want to reimplement this widget if you have been postponing some of the layout / rendering implementation until the latest moment possible. In that case you should make sure you call the base implementation however. 

Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WWebWidget_a5ca222ef9275cfd6d0005c63197d40a0}{Wt\+::\+W\+Web\+Widget}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a59045f8e5af350a4de8b1db9e00b8bb2}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a59045f8e5af350a4de8b1db9e00b8bb2}} 
\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!renderbufferStorage@{renderbufferStorage}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{renderbufferStorage()}{renderbufferStorage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::renderbuffer\+Storage (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ae94560816975bedd91b9d63fc4b710a8}{G\+Lenum}}}]{target,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ae94560816975bedd91b9d63fc4b710a8}{G\+Lenum}}}]{internalformat,  }\item[{unsigned}]{width,  }\item[{unsigned}]{height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\href{http://www.khronos.org/opengles/sdk/2.0/docs/man/xhtml/glRenderbufferStorage.xml}{\texttt{ gl\+Sample\+Coverage() Open\+GL ES manpage}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a18d874bacc0cf315da7c9eff2867314a}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a18d874bacc0cf315da7c9eff2867314a}} 
\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!repaintGL@{repaintGL}}
\index{repaintGL@{repaintGL}!Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{repaintGL()}{repaintGL()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::repaint\+GL (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WFlags}{W\+Flags}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_a654c780ffca1088c837e689332e77288}{G\+L\+Client\+Side\+Renderer}} $>$}]{which }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



\mbox{\hyperlink{classRequest}{Request}} invocation of resize\+GL, paint\+GL and/or update\+GL. 

If invoked with P\+A\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+GL, the client-\/side cached paint function is updated. If invoked with R\+E\+S\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+GL or U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+GL, the code will be executed once.

If invoked with multiple flags set, the order of execution will be \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_afef1be32851001b0c3836975e67d6ad5}{update\+G\+L()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ab44c8692c63dd82a2b5bcf70961319c5}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ab44c8692c63dd82a2b5bcf70961319c5}} 
\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!repaintSlot@{repaintSlot}}
\index{repaintSlot@{repaintSlot}!Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{repaintSlot()}{repaintSlot()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1JSlot}{J\+Slot}}\& Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::repaint\+Slot (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



A Java\+Script slot that repaints the widget when triggered. 

This is useful for client-\/side initiated repaints. You may e.\+g. use this if you write your own client-\/side mouse handler, or if you updated a texture, or if you\textquotesingle{}re playing a video texture. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_abfb8a52fffd71072d98199ef0cd4cd37}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_abfb8a52fffd71072d98199ef0cd4cd37}} 
\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!resize@{resize}}
\index{resize@{resize}!Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{resize()}{resize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::resize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WLength}{W\+Length}} \&}]{width,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WLength}{W\+Length}} \&}]{height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [override]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Resizes the widget. 

Specifies a fixed size for this widget, setting C\+SS {\ttfamily width} and {\ttfamily height} properties. By default a widget has automatic width and height, which sets a size for the widget following C\+SS rules.

When the widget is not managed by a layout manager, the automatic (natural) size of a widget depends on whether they widget is a {\itshape block} or {\itshape inline} widget\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item a {\itshape block} widget takes by default the width of the parent, and the height that it needs based on its contents
\item an {\itshape inline} widget takes the width and height that it needs based on its contents (possibly wrapping over multiple lines). The width and height of an inline widget cannot be changed (by the letter of C\+SS, although most browsers will react to it in varying ways).
\end{DoxyItemize}

When inserted in a layout manager, the size set will be used as a widget\textquotesingle{}s preferred size, but the widget may be given a different size by the layout manager based on available space and stretch factors. The actual size given by a layout manager may be retrieved by making the widget \char`\"{}layout size aware\char`\"{}, using \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WWidget_a4f83592912a7f8fa4fd35dadde78ee74}{set\+Layout\+Size\+Aware()}}. If you have defined a {\ttfamily \char`\"{}wt\+Resize()\char`\"{}} Java\+Script method for the widget, then this method will also be called.

The default width and height of a widget is \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WLength_a0cf39ca4225776879d56ade60320c31a}{W\+Length\+::\+Auto}}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WWebWidget_a3e1a8d2d95fa92763e2e3a0ee520468f}{width()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WWebWidget_ae0c87ae7cae2379eebbbb7df06e07a2c}{height()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WWebWidget_a5113267dfd734df27d4b1c76e7d23abb}{Wt\+::\+W\+Web\+Widget}}.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}} 
\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!resizeGL@{resizeGL}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{resizeGL()}{resizeGL()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::resize\+GL (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{width,  }\item[{int}]{height }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Act on resize events. 

Usually, this method only contains functions to set the viewport and the projection matrix (as this is aspect ration dependent).

\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_af03295d2ebbbff8927acac128e5ae116}{resize\+G\+L()}} is rendered after initialize\+GL, and whenever widget is resized. After this method finishes, the widget is repainted with the cached client-\/side paint function.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a95701ef1dc1da6a694da630daba35b5e}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a95701ef1dc1da6a694da630daba35b5e}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::set\+Alternative\+Content (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WWidget}{W\+Widget}} $>$}]{alternative }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the content to be displayed when Web\+GL is not available. 

If Wt cannot create a working Web\+GL context, this content will be shown to the user. This may be a text explanation, or a pre-\/rendered image, or a video, a flash movie, ...

The default is a widget that explains to the user that he has no Web\+GL support. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ab48ffc7334fd340caa0fd48b6e77f067}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ab48ffc7334fd340caa0fd48b6e77f067}} 
\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!setClientSideLookAtHandler@{setClientSideLookAtHandler}}
\index{setClientSideLookAtHandler@{setClientSideLookAtHandler}!Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setClientSideLookAtHandler()}{setClientSideLookAtHandler()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::set\+Client\+Side\+Look\+At\+Handler (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1JavaScriptMatrix4x4}{Java\+Script\+Matrix4x4}} \&}]{m,  }\item[{double}]{lX,  }\item[{double}]{lY,  }\item[{double}]{lZ,  }\item[{double}]{uX,  }\item[{double}]{uY,  }\item[{double}]{uZ,  }\item[{double}]{pitch\+Rate,  }\item[{double}]{yaw\+Rate }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Add a mouse handler to the widget that looks at a given point. 

This will allow a user to change client-\/side matrix m with the mouse. M is a model transformation matrix, representing the viewpoint of the camera.

Through mouse operations, the camera can be changed by the user, but (lX, lY, lZ) will always be at the center of the display, (uX, uY, uZ) is considered to be the up direction, and the distance of the camera to (lX, lY, lZ) will never change.

Pressing the left mouse button and moving the mouse left/right will rotate the camera around the up (uX, uY, uZ) direction. Moving up/down will tilt the camera (causing it to move up/down to keep the lookpoint centered). The scroll wheel simulates zooming by scaling the scene.

pitch\+Rate and yaw\+Rate control how much the camera will move per mouse pixel.

Usually this method is called after setting a camera transformation with a client-\/side matrix in \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}}. However, this function may also be called from outside the intialize\+G\+L()/paint\+GL()/update\+GL() methods (but not before m was initialized). \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add02e88b9b5359167dbbf16883654bc6}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add02e88b9b5359167dbbf16883654bc6}} 
\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!setClientSideMouseHandler@{setClientSideMouseHandler}}
\index{setClientSideMouseHandler@{setClientSideMouseHandler}!Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setClientSideMouseHandler()}{setClientSideMouseHandler()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::set\+Client\+Side\+Mouse\+Handler (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::string \&}]{handler\+Code }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set a custom mouse handler based on the given Java\+Script code. 

The handler code should be Java\+Script code that produces an object when evaluated.

A mouse handler is an object that can implement one or more of the following functions\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{set\+Target(target)}}\+: This is called immediately when the mouse handler is added with an object that uniquely identifies the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}, and a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a4a29ec70f3803e5b658f2f0f29685e57}{paint\+G\+L()}} method.
\item {\bfseries{mouse\+Down(o, event)}}\+: To handle the {\ttfamily mousedown} event. {\ttfamily o} is the {\ttfamily $<$canvas$>$} (client-\/side rendering) or {\ttfamily $<$img$>$} (server-\/side rendering) element corresponding to this \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}. {\ttfamily event} is the {\ttfamily Mouse\+Event}.
\item {\bfseries{mouse\+Up(o, event)}}\+: To handle the {\ttfamily mouseup} event. {\ttfamily o} is the {\ttfamily $<$canvas$>$} (client-\/side rendering) or {\ttfamily $<$img$>$} (server-\/side rendering) element corresponding to this \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}. {\ttfamily event} is the {\ttfamily Mouse\+Event}.
\item {\bfseries{mouse\+Drag(o, event)}}\+: Called when the mouse is dragged. {\ttfamily o} is the {\ttfamily $<$canvas$>$} (client-\/side rendering) or {\ttfamily $<$img$>$} (server-\/side rendering) element corresponding to this \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}. {\ttfamily event} is the {\ttfamily Mouse\+Event}.
\item {\bfseries{mouse\+Move(o, event)}}\+: Called when the mouse is moved. {\ttfamily o} is the {\ttfamily $<$canvas$>$} (client-\/side rendering) or {\ttfamily $<$img$>$} (server-\/side rendering) element corresponding to this \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}. {\ttfamily event} is the {\ttfamily Mouse\+Event}.
\item {\bfseries{mouse\+Wheel(o, event)}}\+: Called when the mouse wheel is used. {\ttfamily o} is the {\ttfamily $<$canvas$>$} (client-\/side rendering) or {\ttfamily $<$img$>$} (server-\/side rendering) element corresponding to this \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}. {\ttfamily event} is the {\ttfamily Mouse\+Event}.
\item {\bfseries{touch\+Start(o, event)}}\+: To handle the {\ttfamily touchstart} event. {\ttfamily o} is the {\ttfamily $<$canvas$>$} (client-\/side rendering) or {\ttfamily $<$img$>$} (server-\/side rendering) element corresponding to this \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}. {\ttfamily event} is the {\ttfamily Touch\+Event}.
\item {\bfseries{touch\+End(o, event)}}\+: To handle the {\ttfamily touchend} event. {\ttfamily o} is this {\ttfamily $<$canvas$>$} (client-\/side rendering) or {\ttfamily $<$img$>$} (server-\/side rendering) element corresponding to this \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}. {\ttfamily event} is the {\ttfamily Touch\+Event}.
\item {\bfseries{touch\+Moved(o, event)}}\+: To handle the {\ttfamily touchmove} event. {\ttfamily o} is this {\ttfamily $<$canvas$>$} (client-\/side rendering) or {\ttfamily $<$img$>$} (server-\/side rendering) element corresponding to this \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}. {\ttfamily event} is the {\ttfamily Touch\+Event}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

For example, if we wanted to scale some object when we scroll, we could create a \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1JavaScriptMatrix4x4}{Java\+Script\+Matrix4x4}} called {\ttfamily transform\+\_\+\+:} 

We can add this in the constructor\+:

Then, in \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}}, we can initialize it and set the value\+:

Then, still in \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}}, we can set a mouse handler as such\+:

All that\textquotesingle{}s left to do then is to use this transform somewhere as a uniform variable, see \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ac496c003ea91c4138a9e60c727401eac}{get\+Uniform\+Location()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a8236354309932cd6916ba3bde6e85c24}{uniform\+Matrix4()}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a3525a486075289be5d9bc968b0d1fdd1}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a3525a486075289be5d9bc968b0d1fdd1}} 
\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!setClientSideWalkHandler@{setClientSideWalkHandler}}
\index{setClientSideWalkHandler@{setClientSideWalkHandler}!Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setClientSideWalkHandler()}{setClientSideWalkHandler()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::set\+Client\+Side\+Walk\+Handler (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1JavaScriptMatrix4x4}{Java\+Script\+Matrix4x4}} \&}]{m,  }\item[{double}]{front\+Step,  }\item[{double}]{rot\+Step }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Add a mouse handler to the widget that allows \textquotesingle{}walking\textquotesingle{} in the scene. 

This will allow a user to change client-\/side matrix m with the mouse. M is a model transformation matrix, representing the viewpoint of the camera.

Through mouse operations, the camera can be changed by the user, as if he is walking around on a plane.

Pressing the left mouse button and moving the mouse left/right will rotate the camera around Y axis. Moving the mouse up/down will move the camera in the Z direction (walking forward/backward). centered).

front\+Step and rot\+Step control how much the camera will move per mouse pixel. \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ae7406e2b943de20de2b0c6ef2b721495}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ae7406e2b943de20de2b0c6ef2b721495}}

\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!setRenderOptions@{setRenderOptions}}
\index{setRenderOptions@{setRenderOptions}!Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRenderOptions()}{setRenderOptions()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::set\+Render\+Options (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WFlags}{W\+Flags}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_a4629e21e7da64f5597fe3ba70e1729b5}{G\+L\+Render\+Option}} $>$}]{options }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the rendering option. 

Use this method to configure whether client-\/side and/or server-\/side rendering can be used, and whether anti-\/aliasing should be enabled. The actual choice is also based on availability (respectively client-\/side or server-\/side).

The default value is to try both Client\+Side or Server\+Side rendering, and to enable anti-\/aliasing if available.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Options must be set before the widget is being rendered. 
\end{DoxyNote}

GL function to load a 2D texture loaded with \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a6fb55c03c4c43faf5d4372b57ec5d6c4}{create\+Texture\+And\+Load()}} 

This function must only be used for textures created with \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a6fb55c03c4c43faf5d4372b57ec5d6c4}{create\+Texture\+And\+Load()}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classNote}{Note}}\+: the \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}} implementation will delay rendering until all textures created with \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a6fb55c03c4c43faf5d4372b57ec5d6c4}{create\+Texture\+And\+Load()}} are loaded in the browser.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::tex\+Image2D (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ae94560816975bedd91b9d63fc4b710a8}{G\+Lenum}}}]{target,  }\item[{int}]{level,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ae94560816975bedd91b9d63fc4b710a8}{G\+Lenum}}}]{internalformat,  }\item[{unsigned}]{width,  }\item[{unsigned}]{height,  }\item[{int}]{border,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ae94560816975bedd91b9d63fc4b710a8}{G\+Lenum}}}]{format }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



GL function to reserve space for a 2D texture, without specifying its contents. 

This corresponds to calling the Web\+GL function void tex\+Image2D(G\+Lenum target, G\+Lint level, G\+Lenum internalformat, G\+Lsizei width, G\+Lsizei height, G\+Lint border, G\+Lenum format, G\+Lenum type, Array\+Buffer\+View pixels) with null as last parameters. The value of \textquotesingle{}type\textquotesingle{} is then of no importance and is therefore omitted from this function.

\href{http://www.khronos.org/opengles/sdk/2.0/docs/man/xhtml/glTexImage2D.xml}{\texttt{ gl\+Tex\+Image2\+D() Open\+GL ES manpage}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a13f5947600ca36f0f7c887dfbd64f4d3}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_a13f5947600ca36f0f7c887dfbd64f4d3}}

\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!updateGL@{updateGL}}
\index{updateGL@{updateGL}!Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{updateGL()}{updateGL()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily virtual void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::update\+GL (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Update state set in \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_add3bc5d636c0c278e4a4bbaa2d4be445}{initialize\+G\+L()}} 

Invoked when repaint is called with the U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+GL call.

This is intended to be executed when you want to change programs, \textquotesingle{}constant\textquotesingle{} uniforms, or even V\+BO\textquotesingle{}s, ... without resending already initialized data. It is a mechanism to make changes to what you\textquotesingle{}ve set in intialize\+G\+L(). For every server-\/side invocation of this method, the result will be rendered client-\/side exactly once. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1Chart_1_1WCartesian3DChart_abc4076c92139b97ce03ef75110cfb60c}{Wt\+::\+Chart\+::\+W\+Cartesian3\+D\+Chart}}.

\index{Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}!vertexAttribPointer@{vertexAttribPointer}}
\index{vertexAttribPointer@{vertexAttribPointer}!Wt::WGLWidget@{Wt::WGLWidget}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vertexAttribPointer()}{vertexAttribPointer()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Wt\+::\+W\+G\+L\+Widget\+::vertex\+Attrib\+Pointer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_1_1AttribLocation}{Attrib\+Location}}}]{location,  }\item[{int}]{size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_ae94560816975bedd91b9d63fc4b710a8}{G\+Lenum}}}]{type,  }\item[{bool}]{normalized,  }\item[{unsigned}]{stride,  }\item[{unsigned}]{offset }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



GL function to bind a V\+BO to an attribute. 

This function links the given attribute to the V\+BO currently bound to the A\+R\+R\+A\+Y\+\_\+\+B\+U\+F\+F\+ER target.

The size parameter specifies the number of components per attribute (1 to 4). The type parameter is also used to determine the size of each component.

The size of a float is 8 bytes.

In \mbox{\hyperlink{classWt_1_1WGLWidget}{W\+G\+L\+Widget}}, the size of an int is 4 bytes.

The stride is in bytes.

The maximum stride is 255.

\href{http://www.khronos.org/opengles/sdk/2.0/docs/man/xhtml/glVertexAttribPointer.xml}{\texttt{ gl\+Vertex\+Attrib\+Pointer() Open\+GL ES manpage}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_aa7eef06c55522565ae86d9d84ebcbf79}\label{classWt_1_1WGLWidget_aa7eef06c55522565ae86d9d84ebcbf79}}
